     <p>
      <span style="font-size: 120%;">
       <b>
        General characteristics
       </b>
      </span>
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <b>
        Crew:
       </b>
       four (aircraft commander, copilot, offensive systems officer and defensive systems officer)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Payload" title="Payload">
         Payload
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       125,000 lb (56,700 kg); internal and external ordnance combined
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        Length:
       </b>
       146 ft (44.5 m)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Wingspan" title="Wingspan">
         Wingspan
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       <br/>
       <ul>
        <li>
         <b>
          Extended:
         </b>
         137 ft (42m)
        </li>
        <li>
         <b>
          Swept:
         </b>
         79 ft (24m)
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        Height:
       </b>
       34 ft (10.4 m)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        Wing area:
       </b>
       1,950 ft (181.2 m)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Airfoil" title="Airfoil">
         Airfoil
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       <a href="/wiki/NACA_airfoil" title="NACA airfoil">
        NACA69-190-2
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Manufacturer%27s_empty_weight" title="Manufacturer's empty weight">
         Empty weight
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       192,000 lb (87,100 kg)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        Loaded weight:
       </b>
       326,000 lb (148,000 kg)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Maximum_takeoff_weight" title="Maximum takeoff weight">
         Max. takeoff weight
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       477,000 lb (216,400 kg)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Aircraft_engine" title="Aircraft engine">
         Powerplant
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       4 
       <a href="/wiki/General_Electric_F101" title="General Electric F101">
        General Electric F101
       </a>
       -GE-102 augmented
       <a href="/wiki/Turbofan" title="Turbofan">
        turbofans
       </a>
       <ul>
        <li>
         <b>
          Dry thrust:
         </b>
         14,600 lbf (64.9 kN) each
        </li>
        <li>
         <b>
          Thrust with
          <a href="/wiki/Afterburner" title="Afterburner">
           afterburner
          </a>
          :
         </b>
         30,780 lbf (136.92 kN) each
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        Fuel capacity, optional:
       </b>
       10,000 U.S. gal (38,000 L) fuel tank in 13 internal weapons bays each
      </li>
     </ul>
     <p>
      <span style="font-size: 120%;">
       <b>
        Performance
       </b>
      </span>
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/V_speeds#Regulatory_V-speeds" title="V speeds">
         Maximum speed
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       <br/>
       <ul>
        <li>
         <b>
          At altitude:
         </b>
         <a href="/wiki/Mach_number" title="Mach number">
          Mach
         </a>
         1.25 (721kn or 830mph or 1,335km/h) at 50,000ft or 15,000m altitude
        </li>
        <li>
         <b>
          At low level:
         </b>
         Mach 0.92 (700mph or 1,100km/h) at 200500ft or 61152m altitude
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Range_(aeronautics)" title="Range (aeronautics)">
         Range
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       6,478 nmi (7,455mi; 11,997km)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Combat_radius" title="Combat radius">
         Combat radius
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       2,993 nmi (3,444mi; 5,543km)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Ceiling_(aeronautics)" title="Ceiling (aeronautics)">
         Service ceiling
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       60,000 ft (18,000 m)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Wing_loading" title="Wing loading">
         Wing loading
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       167 lb/ft (816 kg/m)
      </li>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Thrust-to-weight_ratio" title="Thrust-to-weight ratio">
         Thrust/weight
        </a>
        :
       </b>
       0.38
      </li>
     </ul>
     <p>
      <span style="font-size: 120%;">
       <b>
        Armament
       </b>
      </span>
      <br/>
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Hardpoint" title="Hardpoint">
         Hardpoints
        </a>

       </b>

       <a href="/wiki/START_I" title="START I">
        arms treaties
       </a>

         <span>
          [
         </span>
         103
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       ) and three internal bomb bays for 75,000 pounds (34,000kg) of ordnance.
      </li>

         </sup>

        </span>

       <li id="cite_note-180">
        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         <b>
          <a href="#cite_ref-180">
           ^
          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         As per B-1B Weapons Loading Checklist T.O. 1B-1B-33-2-1CL-13
        </span>
       </li>
       <li id="cite_note-181">
        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         <b>
          <a href="#cite_ref-181">
           ^
          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         both Mk-84 general purpose and
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BLU-109" title="BLU-109">
          BLU-109
         </a>
         penetrating bombs
        </span>
       </li>
       <li id="cite_note-182">
        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         <b>
          <a href="#cite_ref-182">
           ^
          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         As per B-1B Weapons Loading Checklist T.O. 1B-1B-33-2-1CL-12 Section 3.4 (Only six each in forward and intermediate bays and three each in the aft bay)
        </span>
       </li>
       <li id="cite_note-184">
        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         <b>
          <a href="#cite_ref-184">
           ^
          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         96 if using four-packs, 144 if using six-packs. This capability has not yet been fielded on the B-1
        </span>
       </li>
      </ol>
